\DoxyCodeLine{00726\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01356\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Routing\ policies\ for\ Shortcut()\ +\ low-\/level\ SetShortcutRouting()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01357\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ The\ general\ idea\ is\ that\ several\ callers\ register\ interest\ in\ a\ shortcut,\ and\ only\ one\ owner\ gets\ it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01358\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ When\ a\ policy\ (other\ than\ \_RouteAlways)\ is\ set,\ Shortcut()\ will\ register\ itself\ with\ SetShortcutRouting(),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01359\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ allowing\ the\ system\ to\ decide\ where\ to\ route\ the\ input\ among\ other\ route-\/aware\ calls.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01360\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Shortcut()\ uses\ ImGuiInputFlags\_RouteFocused\ by\ default:\ meaning\ that\ a\ simple\ Shortcut()\ poll}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01361\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ will\ register\ a\ route\ and\ only\ succeed\ when\ parent\ window\ is\ in\ the\ focus\ stack\ and\ if\ no-\/one}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01362\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ with\ a\ higher\ priority\ is\ claiming\ the\ shortcut.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01363\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Using\ ImGuiInputFlags\_RouteAlways\ is\ roughly\ equivalent\ to\ doing\ e.g.\ IsKeyPressed(key)\ +\ testing\ mods.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01364\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Priorities:\ GlobalHigh\ >\ Focused\ (when\ owner\ is\ active\ item)\ >\ Global\ >\ Focused\ (when\ focused\ window)\ >\ GlobalLow.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01365\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Can\ select\ only\ 1\ policy\ among\ all\ available.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01366\ \ \ \ \ ImGuiInputFlags\_RouteFocused\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 1\ <<\ 8,\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ (Default)\ Register\ focused\ route:\ Accept\ inputs\ if\ window\ is\ in\ focus\ stack.\ Deep-\/most\ focused\ window\ takes\ inputs.\ ActiveId\ takes\ inputs\ over\ deep-\/most\ focused\ window.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01367\ \ \ \ \ ImGuiInputFlags\_RouteGlobalLow\ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 1\ <<\ 9,\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Register\ route\ globally\ (lowest\ priority:\ unless\ a\ focused\ window\ or\ active\ item\ registered\ the\ route)\ -\/>\ recommended\ Global\ priority.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01368\ \ \ \ \ ImGuiInputFlags\_RouteGlobal\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ =\ 1\ <<\ 10,\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Register\ route\ globally\ (medium\ priority:\ unless\ an\ active\ item\ registered\ the\ route,\ e.g.\ CTRL+A\ registered\ by\ InputText).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01369\ \ \ \ \ ImGuiInputFlags\_RouteGlobalHigh\ \ \ \ \ =\ 1\ <<\ 11,\ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Register\ route\ globally\ (highest\ priority:\ unlikely\ you\ need\ to\ use\ that:\ will\ interfere\ with\ every\ active\ items)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{02910\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ [EXPERIMENTAL]\ Low-\/Level:\ Key/Input\ Ownership}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02911\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ The\ idea\ is\ that\ instead\ of\ "{}eating"{}\ a\ given\ input,\ we\ can\ link\ to\ an\ owner\ id.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02912\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Ownership\ is\ most\ often\ claimed\ as\ a\ result\ of\ reacting\ to\ a\ press/down\ event\ (but\ occasionally\ may\ be\ claimed\ ahead).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02913\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Input\ queries\ can\ then\ read\ input\ by\ specifying\ ImGuiKeyOwner\_Any\ (==\ 0),\ ImGuiKeyOwner\_None\ (==\ -\/1)\ or\ a\ custom\ ID.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02914\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Legacy\ input\ queries\ (without\ specifying\ an\ owner\ or\ \_Any\ or\ \_None)\ are\ equivalent\ to\ using\ ImGuiKeyOwner\_Any\ (==\ 0).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02915\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ Input\ ownership\ is\ automatically\ released\ on\ the\ frame\ after\ a\ key\ is\ released.\ Therefore:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02916\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ -\/\ for\ ownership\ registration\ happening\ as\ a\ result\ of\ a\ down/press\ event,\ the\ SetKeyOwner()\ call\ may\ be\ done\ once\ (common\ case).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02917\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ -\/\ for\ ownership\ registration\ happening\ ahead\ of\ a\ down/press\ event,\ the\ SetKeyOwner()\ call\ needs\ to\ be\ made\ every\ frame\ (happens\ if\ e.g.\ claiming\ ownership\ on\ hover).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02918\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ SetItemKeyOwner()\ is\ a\ shortcut\ for\ common\ simple\ case.\ A\ custom\ widget\ will\ probably\ want\ to\ call\ SetKeyOwner()\ multiple\ times\ directly\ based\ on\ its\ interaction\ state.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02919\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ This\ is\ marked\ experimental\ because\ not\ all\ widgets\ are\ fully\ honoring\ the\ Set/Test\ idioms.\ We\ will\ need\ to\ move\ forward\ step\ by\ step.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02920\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ Please\ open\ a\ GitHub\ Issue\ to\ submit\ your\ usage\ scenario\ or\ if\ there's\ a\ use\ case\ you\ need\ solved.}}
